Get Booking Ids

  Under 1 Second (Duration)

Get list of booking IDs
 

Cast

  Tester

Tester can:
  • browse the web
  • call an API at https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com

Scenario Outline

Given the actor wants to retrieve booking IDs with "<filter>"
When the actor sends the request to get booking IDs
Then the response status code should be 200
And the booking IDs list should not be empty

Examples: 

# Filter
1
2 firstname=Josh&lastname=Allen
3 checkin=2018-01-01&checkout=2019-01-01
